### Round 5: San Marino Grand Prix
*Date: 1992-05-17*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |

### Round 13: Italian Grand Prix
*Date: 1992-09-13*

#### Qualifying Results

| Driver | Constructor | Grid | Status | Starting ELO | Change | New ELO | vs Teammate |
